Conclusion: 跨司法管辖区法律NLP评估存在巨大差异，模型架构和预训练数据比分词器效率更重要，需要更细粒度的跨语言评估方法。

Abstract: Legal NLP benchmarks overwhelmingly evaluate a single language or aggregate tasks that differ fundamentally across jurisdictions, making cross-lingual comparison impossible. We introduce Multi-Legal-Bench, the first cross-jurisdictional legal benchmark that evaluates identical tasks across six countries (Ukraine, France, Netherlands, Poland, Czech Republic, Lithuania), four language families, and 134 million court decisions. The benchmark defines five tasks court-type classification, judgment form classification, case-outcome prediction, legal norm extraction, and cause category prediction mapped to structured metadata from national court registries, forming a deliberately sparse 5x6 task-jurisdiction matrix (20 of 30 cells filled). We evaluate 7 frontier LLMs under zero-shot and 3-shot prompting via AWS Bedrock, with 4 additional small/medium models (3-12B) for scaling analysis. Our results reveal that: (1) task-dependent few-shot effects discovered in Ukrainian replicate across all jurisdictions; (2) no single model dominates any language rankings shift with both task and jurisdiction; (3) cross-lingual few-shot transfer does not follow language proximity: UA->FR (Romance, -2.1 pp) transfers better than UA->PL (Slavic, -13.7 pp), with label-set alignment predicting transfer quality better than language family; and (4) tokenizer fertility, despite a 2.3x spread, does not significantly predict cross-lingual accuracy (r=-0.27, p=0.14), suggesting that model architecture and pretraining data dominate tokenizer efficiency. We release all data, prompts, and model predictions.

### [189] [DySem: Uncovering Dynamic Semantic Components via Multilingual Consensus for Calculating Semantic Textual Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29751)
*Kaijie Zheng,Weiqin Wang,Yile Wang,Hui Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DySem提出了一种无需训练的新框架，通过多语言共识挖掘LLM中更语义相关的内部组件，并构建文本依赖的动态语义维度子集来计算语义文本相似度，在降低维度的同时一致优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的语义文本相似度计算方法存在两个局限：(1) 最后一层隐藏层编码的是通用知识而非纯语义知识，不适用于语义相似度计算；(2) LLM隐藏层维度很大，包含冗余和噪声。因此需要探索更语义相关的内部表示和动态语义维度。

Method: 提出DySem框架：(1) 通过多语言共识（multilingual consensus）挖掘LLM中与语义更相关的内部组件（而非仅用最后一层）；(2) 构建文本依赖的联合语义集（text-dependent joint semantic set），为每对文本动态选择共享的语义维度子集，在此降维后的共享维度空间上计算相似度。该方法无需训练。

Result: 在多种LLM上的大量实验表明，DySem在降低相似度计算维度的同时，一致性地优于近期基线方法。

Conclusion: 通过利用多语言共识定位语义相关内部组件并动态选择样本特定的语义维度，可以更高效、更准确地计算语义文本相似度，无需额外训练。

Abstract: Calculating semantic textual similarity is a foundational task in natural language processing. Current large language models (LLMs) based methods typically rely on extracting last-layer hidden states with fixed dimensions to compute similarity for every text pairs. We argue that this paradigm is suffer from two limitations: (i) The last hidden layer encodes more general knowledge rather than just semantic knowledge, making it suboptimal for semantic similarity computation; (ii) The hidden layer dimensions of LLMs are generally very large, which introduces some redundancy and noise for representing semantics. In this work, we propose DySem, a novel training-free framework that investigates more semantic-related internal components of LLMs via multilingual consensus, and shifts away from static representation spaces in favor of dynamic, sample-specific semantic dimensions by constructing text-dependent joint semantic set and computes similarity over this shared dimensional subset. Extensive experiments across various LLMs show that our method consistently outperforms recent baselines while maintaining lower dimensions for similarity calculation. The code is released at https://github.com/szu-tera/DySem.

### [190] [ActTraitBench: Quantifying the Knowledge-Decision Gap in Large Language Models via Human-Grounded Behavioral Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29791)
*Yutong Yang,Chenxi Miao,Weikang Li,Yunfang Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出ActTraitBench框架评估LLM的人格一致性，发现知识-决策差距（$G_{\text{KD}}$），即模型在自陈报告中能模拟人格但在行为决策中偏离；并引入CoCA方法在推理阶段缩小该差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准难以测量LLM在自陈报告与行为决策之间的人格不对称性，因为存在构念效度有限、多维度纠缠以及基于LLM评估的分布偏差等问题。

Method: 1) 基于人类经验数据建立心理测量学维度与行为范式的一对一映射；2) 采用分位数映射的分布校准方法使LLM评判者的评分分布与人类规范对齐；3) 提出链式认知对齐（CoCA）作为推理时干预手段。

Result: 在14个主流LLM上发现普遍的知识-决策不对称：更大、能力更强的模型尽管自陈报告高度一致，但行为分歧更显著；CoCA能改善推理型前沿模型的对齐，但在小架构上暴露能力局限。

Conclusion: LLM存在系统性的知识-决策差距，需通过推理时认知对齐等方法加以缓解；当前模型规模与行为一致性之间并非单调正相关。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) can convincingly simulate personas in explicit self-reports, they often deviate in implicit behavioral decisions, revealing a substantial Knowledge-Decision Gap ($G_{\text{KD}}$). Existing benchmarks struggle to measure this asymmetry due to limited construct validity, multi-dimensional entanglement, and distributional biases in LLM-based evaluation. To address these issues, we propose ActTraitBench, a human-grounded evaluation framework for measuring personality consistency in LLMs. Grounded in empirical human data, ActTraitBench establishes one-to-one mappings between psychometric facets and behavioral paradigms, and applies a Distributional Calibration via Quantile Mapping procedure to align LLM-judge score distributions with human norms. Experiments on 14 mainstream LLMs reveal a pervasive knowledge-decision asymmetry, where larger and more capable models often exhibit stronger behavioral divergence despite highly consistent self-reports. To mitigate this gap, we further introduce the Chain of Cognitive Alignment (CoCA), a plug-and-play inference-time intervention that improves alignment in reasoning-capable frontier models while exposing clear capability limitations in smaller architectures.

### [191] [Metric-Dependent Annotation Saturation for Learning from Label Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29797)
*Guneet Kohli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究标注不一致信号与评估指标的关系，发现软标签（N~20-50）在熵相关性上优于标签平滑（r=0.643 vs 0.45-0.49），而KL散度在N~10时已饱和，建议标注预算应根据目标评估指标设定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究标注者之间的分歧信号如何被有效捕捉，以及所需标注者数量如何依赖于具体的评估指标，从而为标注预算分配提供理论依据。

Method: 使用ChaosNLI数据集（每项100个独立标注）对NLI模型进行标签分布微调，对比软标签与标签平滑在不同标注者数量（N）下对熵相关性和KL散度的影响，并在DeBERTa、RoBERTa等架构上验证。

Result: 熵相关性需要N~20-50才能收敛，而KL散度在N~10时已饱和（87-95%改进）。软标签的熵相关性（r=0.643）显著优于标签平滑（r=0.45-0.49），后者无法区分歧义项与清晰项。该优势跨架构和数据域保持一致。

Conclusion: 标注预算应根据目标评估指标差异化设定，而非统一标准；软标签比标签平滑更能捕捉标注者分歧中的项目特定信号。

Abstract: When annotators disagree on a label, the disagreement itself carries signal -- and the number of annotators needed to capture it depends on the evaluation metric. We fine-tune NLI models on label distributions subsampled from ChaosNLI, a dataset providing 100 independent annotator judgments per item, and identify metric-dependent saturation. In our 3-class NLI setting, entropy correlation -- whether the model identifies which items elicit disagreement -- requires N ~ 20-50 annotators to converge, while distributional match (KL divergence) saturates by N ~ 10 (87-95% of improvement across five model seeds). This finding rests on a prior observation: soft labels carry item-specific signal that label smoothing cannot replicate. Across five smoothing intensities, entropy correlation clusters at r ~ 0.45-0.49, while soft labels reach r = 0.643 (p < 0.001); per-item analysis traces this gap to smoothing's inability to distinguish ambiguous items from clear ones. The soft-label advantage replicates across two architectures (DeBERTa, RoBERTa), a non-NLI-pretrained baseline, and an exploratory cross-domain evaluation on content safety. These results suggest that annotation budgets should be informed by the target evaluation metric rather than set uniformly.

### [192] [Nine Judges, Two Effective Votes: Correlated Errors Undermine LLM Evaluation Panels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29800)
*Guneet Kohli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLM评审小组中多个模型的投票看似独立，但实际上约75%的信息是冗余的，9个前沿模型仅提供约2个独立投票的信息量，导致实际准确率比理想独立投票低8-22个百分点，增加法官数量或改进聚合算法都无法解决这一瓶颈，根本问题在于模型之间的高相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化LLM-as-a-judge评审小组中法官之间的真实信息独立性，揭示其与理想独立投票假设之间的差距。

Method: 采用Kish有效样本量(n_eff)和Condorcet零模型框架，测试9个来自7个模型家族的前沿LLM在3个自然语言推理数据集上的表现（每个数据点100个人工标注），并验证了提示变体、温度、思维链推理和成对偏好任务(RewardBench)下的鲁棒性。

Result: 9个法官仅提供约2个独立投票的信息量；约四分之三的名义独立性因模型在相同项目上犯相同错误而丢失；实际准确率比独立投票低8-22个百分点；最佳单一法官在所有条件下均达到或超过整个评审小组；即使使用正确答案，已建立的聚合方法也只能缩小最多11%的差距。

Conclusion: 评审小组的瓶颈在于法官之间的高相关性而非聚合算法，扩大评审规模无法替代真正独立的评估。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-judge panels aggregate votes from multiple models, with the expectation that diverse models yield more reliable evaluations. We develop a framework to measure the true informational value of such panels and quantify how far their reliability falls short of the independent-voting ideal. Testing a panel of 9 frontier LLMs from 7 model families on three natural language inference datasets (each with 100 human annotations per item), we find that the 9 judges effectively provide only about 2 independent votes' worth of information. Roughly three-quarters of the panel's nominal independence is lost because the models make the same mistakes on the same items. The consequences are stark: the panel's actual accuracy falls 8-22 percentage points short of what independent voting would achieve, and the best single judge matches or outperforms the full panel across all conditions. Neither adding more judges nor using smarter aggregation algorithms helps -- established methods close at most 11% of this gap, even with access to the correct answers. We quantify these findings using the Kish effective sample size (n_eff) and a Condorcet null model, and show the deficit is robust across prompt variants, temperatures, chain-of-thought reasoning, and a pairwise preference task (RewardBench). The bottleneck is correlated judges, not the aggregation algorithm, implying that scaling up panels cannot substitute for genuinely independent evaluation.

### [193] [Data filtering methods for training language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29807)
*Egor Shevchenko,Elena Bruches*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文比较了Confident Learning和Dataset Cartography两种自动标签错误检测方法在三个俄语文本分类数据集上的效果，发现其有效性高度依赖数据集特性：在大规模低噪声数据集上过滤无益，而在小规模高噪声数据集上Confident Learning能显著提升F1-macro分数，两种方法均优于随机移除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据质量对机器学习模型效果至关重要，标签错误即使在广泛使用的基准数据集中也存在，会引入噪声并降低模型泛化能力，因此需要有效的方法自动检测并过滤标签错误。

Method: 在三个不同规模、类别数和领域的俄语文本分类语料库（ru_emotion_e-culture 49,123样本、RuCoLA 8,524样本、TERRa 2,337样本）上，采用预训练的rubert-base-cased模型微调，比较Confident Learning和Dataset Cartography两种标签错误检测方法的效果，并以随机移除等量样本作为对照实验。

Result: 两种方法的效果高度依赖于数据集特征：大规模低噪声数据集上过滤不提升性能，小规模高噪声数据集上Confident Learning显著提升F1-macro；Dataset Cartography更保守，移除样本更少；两种方法的针对性移除均优于随机移除。

Conclusion: 标签错误检测方法的有效性因数据集特性而异，在大规模低噪声数据集中过滤无益，但在小规模高噪声数据集中Confident Learning效果显著，且两种方法对错误样本的定向移除具有实际意义。

Abstract: Data quality is a critical factor in the effectiveness of machine learning models. Label errors, present even in widely used benchmarks, introduce noise into training data and reduce model generalization. In this work, we conduct a comparative analysis of two automatic label error detection methods - Confident Learning and Dataset Cartography - on three Russian text classification corpora of varying size, number of classes, and domain: ru_emotion_e-culture (49,123 examples, emotion classification), RuCoLA (8,524 examples, linguistic acceptability), and TERRa (2,337 examples, textual entailment recognition). We use the pre-trained rubert-base-cased model fine-tuned on each corpus. To verify the meaningfulness of filtering, we conduct control experiments with random removal of an equivalent number of examples. Results show that the effectiveness of both methods depends strongly on dataset characteristics: on large corpora with low noise levels, filtering does not improve performance, while on small datasets with high noise, Confident Learning achieves a significant F1-macro improvement. Dataset Cartography demonstrates more conservative behavior, removing fewer examples. Across all corpora, targeted removal by both methods outperforms random removal, confirming the meaningfulness of the approaches.

### [194] [Towards Localized and Disentangled Knowledge Editing for Multimodal Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29826)
*Leijiang Gu,Zhen Zeng,Feng Li,Xinjian Gao,Zenglin Shi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出LDKE框架，通过快速定位关键层和解耦分类器，解决多模态知识编辑中因果错位和特征纠缠导致的编辑泛化性差和无关信息干扰问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MKE方法虽能修正错误事实，但存在两个关键局限：编辑无法泛化到逻辑相关查询，且会意外篡改视觉或语义上关联但无关的信息。作者将其归结为因果错位（编辑局限于特定样本）和特征纠缠（无关耦合信息被连带修改）两种失效模式。

Method: 提出LDKE框架，包含两个核心模块：1) 快速定位模块（Fast Localization），识别并高效更新关键层；2) 解耦分类器（Disentanglement Classifier），根据输入路由至合适路径以保留无关知识。通过定位事实特定层和解耦目标相关与无关输入，实现精确且泛化的编辑。

Result: 在多个基准和MLLM上的实验表明，LDKE在将编辑传播到相关上下文方面表现优异，同时保持高度的局部性（不干扰无关知识）。

Conclusion: LDKE通过解耦定位策略有效解决了MKE中编辑泛化性和局部性之间的权衡问题。

Abstract: Existing methods in Multimodal Knowledge Editing (MKE) have advanced the ability to correct outdated or inaccurate knowledge in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). However, they exhibit a critical limitation: while effectively modifying target factual pairs, they fail to generalize edits to logically related queries and often cause unintended alterations to unrelated but visually or semantically linked information. We identify and formalize two underlying failure modes causing this issue: Causal Misalignment, which confines edits to the specific sample, and Feature Entanglement, which causes unintended alterations to coupled but irrelevant information. To address these issues, we propose Localized and Disentangled Knowledge Editing (LDKE), a new framework that achieves precise and generalized editing by localizing fact-specific model layers and disentangling target-relevant inputs from irrelevant ones. Our approach introduces a Fast Localization module to identify and update critical layers efficiently, along with a Disentanglement Classifier that routes inputs appropriately to preserve unrelated knowledge. Extensive experiments across various benchmarks and MLLMs demonstrate that LDKE achieves superior performance in propagating edits to related contexts while maintaining high locality.

</details>


### [195] [EvoRubric: Self-Evolving Rubric-Driven RL for Open-Ended Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29847)
*Xin Guan,Xiaomeng Hu,Shen Huang,Zhenyi Wang,Bo Zhang,Zijian Li,Pengjun Xie,Bo Liu,Jiuxin Cao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在医疗、写作和科学领域的广泛实验中，EvoRubric持续优于传统静态和外部LLM驱动的对齐方法；兼容人类专家先验，初始化后可发现新的判别维度，超越仅依赖静态专家标注的性能。

Current rubric-based RL methods mitigate this by employing explicit criteria; however, they rely heavily on static, human-annotated rubrics that inevitably cause policy lag, or expensive external proprietary models for dynamic updates. In this paper, we propose EvoRubric, a novel single-policy co-evolutionary RL framework that eliminates the reliance on static criteria and on external rubric generators. By unifying response generation and rubric generation under a single parameterized policy, EvoRubric dynamically alternates between a Reasoner and a Rubric Generator. To prevent reward hacking and ensure the reliability of generated signals, we introduce a multi-level verification pipeline featuring a meta-verifier, zero-variance pruning, and a Leave-One-Out peer consensus mechanism. Validated criteria are dynamically archived into a memory pool, yielding dense, multi-objective rewards to continuously co-optimize both roles. Extensive experiments across Medical, Writing, and Science domains demonstrate that EvoRubric consistently outperforms traditional static and external-LLM-driven alignment methods. Notably, our framework is compatible with human-expert priors. When initialized with expert-annotated rubrics, EvoRubric can further uncover novel, discriminative dimensions, achieving better performance than relying solely on static expert annotations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG方法仍存在幻觉和推理错误；外部批评者提供的反馈粗粒度、结构化弱、过度激进干预，导致修正效果有限。

Method: 将RAG批评建模为显式错误诊断问题，划分为裁决、错误位置、推理分析、修正生成四个维度；设计Conservative Judgement Alignment（CJA）奖励函数校准高层级判断以缓解过度干预，Diagnostic Quality Alignment（DQA）奖励函数通过门控奖励提升细粒度诊断反馈；使用GRPO强化学习结合外部LLM教师模型的过程级监督训练批评模型。

Conclusion: 结构化批评框架结合强化学习能有效提升RAG系统的纠错能力，缓解过度干预问题，提供更精细可靠的诊断反馈。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) improves knowledge-intensive question answering by incorporating external evidence. However, existing RAG methods still suffer from hallucinations and subtle reasoning errors. Recent studies introduce external critics to refine RAG outputs, yet they often provide coarse-grained and weakly structured feedback, exhibit over-aggressive intervention, and lead to noisy and unreliable refinement, limiting their effectiveness for correction. To tackle these issues, we propose CRITIC-R1, a structured critic framework that formulates and learns RAG critique as an explicit error diagnosis problem using reinforcement learning (RL). Our framework categorizes common RAG errors into multiple diagnostic dimensions, including verdict, error location, reasoning analysis, and fix generation. To learn these capabilities, we design two reward functions: Conservative Judgement Alignment (CJA) first encourages calibrated high-level judgements while mitigating the over-aggressive phenomenon, whereas Diagnostic Quality Alignment (DQA) further improves fine-grained diagnostic feedback through gated rewards. We train the critic model using GRPO-based RL with process-level supervision collected from external LLM teacher models. Experiments across five QA benchmarks show that CRITIC-R1 consistently improves answer quality over strong RAG baselines.
  Our source code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/critic-r1-FCB0

### [197] [Internal Representation, Not Clinical Knowledge: Where Apparent LLM Triage Failures Originate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29889)
*David Fraile Navarro,Berardino Como,Jialei Sheng,Soundariya Ananthan,Shlomo Berkovsky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文发现，大型语言模型在临床分诊任务中，不同输出格式（多项选择 vs. 自由文本）会导致不同的评分结果。通过稀疏自编码器分析，模型在两种格式下对临床叙事的内部表征是相同的，但在多项选择的决策token处医学特征会“沉默”，而格式和支架特征主导了决策logits。行为分析表明，多项选择的惩罚源于格式本身而非知识缺失，主要表现为“差一位”决策偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究患者叙述的临床分诊基准中，消费级LLM在不同输出格式（多项选择与自由文本）下表现差异的根本原因——即这种差异是源于模型临床表征的改变，还是仅源于从保留的表征到答案映射的变化。

Method: 使用Gemma 3 4B/12B IT和Qwen3-8B模型，结合稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征分析；采用三种独立方法验证：自然语言自编码器口头化、决策token的logit归因、以及顶部特征表征；同时进行行为实验（结构化与自然语言输入下的多项选择惩罚反转、选项顺序洗牌消除位置偏差）。

Result: 医学特征在两种输出格式下对共享临床叙事均有激活，但在多项选择的决策token处所有模型的所有案例中均“沉默”；支架和格式特征（而非医学特征）驱动了决策logits；行为上，多项选择惩罚在结构化与自然语言输入下均发生反转，选项顺序洗牌排除了位置偏差，且差距主要由“差一位”决策（选择相邻严重程度字母）而非知识失败主导。

Conclusion: LLM在临床分诊任务中的多项选择表现欠佳，根源在于输出格式问题而非临床表征问题。模型保留了正确的临床知识，但输出格式限制导致其无法正确映射到多项选择答案。

Abstract: Patient-voiced clinical-triage benchmarks report high under-triage rates for consumer LLMs for constrained multiple-choice output, yet the same cases score differently with free-text. We ask whether output format changes the model's \emph{clinical representation} or only the mapping from a preserved representation to an answer. Using sparse-autoencoder (SAE) features in Gemma 3 4B/12B IT and Qwen3-8B, we find the same medical features fire on the shared clinical narrative under both formats but go {silent} at the multiple-choice decision token in all the cases at every model. Three independent methods (natural-language autoencoder verbalization, decision-token logit attribution, and top-feature characterization) agree that scaffold and format features, but not medical features, drive the decision logits. Behaviorally, the multiple-choice penalty inverts under both structured and natural-language input, option-order shuffle rules out positional bias, and the gap is dominated by off-by-one decision (the model picks an adjacent acuity letter to the gold answer) rather than knowledge failure. Thus, the failure originates in the output format and not in the clinical representation.

### [199] [Causal Interventions on Continuous Variables: A Case Study on Verb Bias in Steering Vectors for In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29971)
*Zhenghao Herbert Zhou,R. Thomas McCoy,Robert Frank*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对语言模型表示中连续变量进行因果干预的方法，通过寻找与连续目标变量（如动词偏向）相关的低维方向向量，并对激活向量进行反事实编辑。实验表明，该方向向量对动词偏向具有因果影响，并能系统性地改变下游句法结构偏好。进一步分析发现，这些方向向量也编码了与上下文学习相关的误差信号，但这些信号在下游生成中并未被因果利用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果干预方法主要针对离散特征（如语法数），但语言模型也需要处理连续型特征。作者希望将因果干预扩展到连续变量，从而更全面地理解模型内部表示机制。

Method: 给定激活向量对和连续的梯度目标变量，定位一个低维方向向量，并利用该方向对激活向量进行反事实目标值的编辑。将该方法应用于动词偏向这一连续特征，该特征反映动词后倾向于出现的句法结构。

Result: （1）反事实编辑动词偏向方向向量能系统性地改变模型下游的句法结构偏好，证明该方向具有因果作用；（2）该方向向量也编码了可能与上下文学习相关的误差信号，但这些信号在下游生成中并未被因果性地利用。

Conclusion: 因果干预可以扩展到连续变量，但将连续变量与上下文学习机制建立因果联系仍面临挑战。

Abstract: Causal interventions in language model representations have largely targeted discrete features, like grammatical number. However, language models must also make use of features that are graded. We introduce a method for causal intervention on continuous variables: given activation vectors paired with a graded target variable, we localize a low-dimensional direction for that variable and use this direction to edit a vectors toward counterfactual target values. We apply this method to a continuous feature that is well-studied in psycholinguistics, namely verb bias (which reflects which syntactic structures tend to follow a given verb). We show that verb bias is causally represented in steering vectors extracted from large language models: counterfactual edits to verb bias systematically shift downstream structural preferences. Verb bias has also previously been linked to in-context learning; in further analyses, we find that steering vectors encode error signals that could drive the error-driven update behavior seen in in-context learning but that these aspects of the steering vectors are not causally used in downstream production. Overall, these results show causal interventions can be applied to continuous variables, though connecting continuous variables to in-context learning remains a challenge.

### [200] [Adapting Multilingual Embedding Models to Turkish via Cross-Lingual Tokenizer Surgery and Offline Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29992)
*M. Ali Bayram,Banu Diri,Savaş Yıldırım*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出embeddingmagibu-200m，一个面向土耳其语的句子嵌入模型，通过三阶段适配管道（分词器优化、教师模型克隆、离线嵌入蒸馏）在单GPU上约4小时训练完成，参数量200M，在STSbTR上超越300M教师模型，实现了成本与性能的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的土耳其语句子嵌入模型受限于512 token的上下文窗口和有限的多语言覆盖，且从头预训练成本高昂。需要一种高效、低成本的方案来构建支持长上下文、高性能的土耳其语专用嵌入模型。

Method: 三阶段适配管道：(1) 基于40语料库的频率分析，从教师模型词表中剪枝冗余token并融入多语言token，构建土耳其语优化的131,072词汇多语言分词器；(2) 克隆教师嵌入模型，保留Transformer骨干权重，通过均值组合token映射初始化新词表的嵌入表；(3) 对平衡的40语言Wikipedia语料库使用余弦相似度目标，基于预计算教师向量进行离线嵌入蒸馏，避免在线教师推理。

Result: 在STSbTR上达到77.55%/77.45%的Pearson/Spearman相关系数，超越300M参数的教师模型(73.84%/72.92%)；在TR-MTEB(26个任务)上平均得分63.9%，在26个模型中位列第7；参数量仅200M，比教师模型少33%。

Conclusion: 提出的三阶段适配管道能够高效地将通用多语言嵌入模型适配到特定语言（土耳其语），在显著降低训练成本（单GPU约4小时，$5-$20）的同时获得更优或接近的性能，为资源受限场景下的语言模型适配提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Sentence embeddings are a foundational component for semantic search, clustering, classification, and retrieval-augmented generation. This paper presents embeddingmagibu-200m, a Turkish-focused sentence embedding model that produces 768-dimensional L2-normalized vectors and supports an 8,192-token context window, far exceeding the 512-token limit of earlier BERT-based Turkish encoders. Instead of full pretraining, an efficient three-stage adaptation pipeline is introduced: (1) construct a Turkish-optimized multilingual tokenizer with a 131,072 vocabulary by pruning redundant tokens from the teacher's vocabulary and incorporating multilingual tokens via frequency analysis on a 40-language corpus, (2) clone a teacher embedding model while preserving transformer backbone weights and initializing a compatible embedding table for the new vocabulary via mean-composition token mapping, and (3) perform offline embedding distillation from precomputed teacher vectors using a cosine similarity objective over a balanced 40-language Wikipedia corpus. The resulting student model contains approximately 200M parameters and trains in roughly four hours on a single GPU by avoiding online teacher inference during training, at a total cost of $5-$20. Empirically, Pearson/Spearman correlations of 77.55%/77.45% are obtained on STSbTR, surpassing the 300M-parameter teacher model (73.84%/72.92%). On TR-MTEB (26 tasks), a mean score of 63.9% is achieved (7th out of 26 models), providing a competitive cost-quality trade-off with 33% fewer parameters than the teacher. To facilitate reproducibility and downstream use, all artifacts are released including model weights, tokenizer files, precomputed embedding datasets, and open-source cloning and distillation tooling.

### [201] [Latent Performance Profiling of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30018)
*Tanmoy Chakraborty,Ayan Sengupta,Suparna Bhattacharya,Partha Pratim Chakrabarti,Amlan Chakrabarti,Supratik Chakraborty,Partha Pratim Das,Lipika Dey,Richa Singh,Mayank Vatsa*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出潜在性能剖析（LPP）框架，从隐藏激活和输出分布中提取任务无关的诊断指标，以补充传统基准评估的不足。在8个0.5B-14B的LLM上实验表明，LPP能揭示基准分数相似模型间在熵、适应性等潜在特征上的差异，提供更深入、可解释的模型行为理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准评估仅关注模型在固定测试集上的输出，无法反映模型如何处理信息、校准不确定性或组织内部知识，且存在数据污染、任务范围狭窄、与真实可靠性对齐弱等问题。

Method: 提出Latent Performance Profiling (LPP)框架，从隐藏激活和输出分布中定义一组标量度量，刻画模型潜在表征和动态特性，实现任务无关的、规模无关的可解释比较。

Result: 在8个LLM（0.5B-14B）上实验发现，基准分数相似的模型在潜在指标（如熵、适应性）上存在显著差异；基于LPP洞察设计的合成探针与内在度量一致，且不受排行榜偏差影响。

Conclusion: 建议在基准评估之外报告LPP，以获得对模型行为更深层、可解释的理解，支持更可靠的模型选择、安全评估和超越表面准确率的评价。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) frequently achieve impressive scores on standardized benchmarks, yet accuracy alone offers a limited view of their capabilities. Evaluating open-source LLMs through leaderboards faces persistent issues like data contamination, narrow task scope, and weak alignment with real-world reliability. Benchmark-based evaluations such as MMLU PRO, BBH, or IFEval primarily capture \textit{what} a model outputs on fixed test sets, not \textit{how} it processes information, calibrates uncertainty, or structures internal knowledge. In this article, we advocate for a shift from benchmark-centric evaluation toward a complementary, \textit{state-centered intrinsic assessment} of LLMs. To this end, we introduce \textbf{Latent Performance Profiling (LPP)} -- a framework that derives task-agnostic diagnostics from hidden activations and output distributions. LPP defines a set of scalar metrics on a model's latent representations and dynamics, revealing scale-independent traits that enable interpretable comparisons and uncover hidden vulnerabilities. Unlike static accuracy scores, LPP provides stable, architecture-sensitive signatures across models of similar size. With extensive empirical analyses across eight LLMs, spanning a size range of 0.5B-14B, we demonstrate that models with similar benchmark scores can exhibit contrasting latent profiles, such as differences in entropy or adaptability. Guided by these insights, we design synthetic probes for uncertainty and symbolic reasoning that align with intrinsic metrics while decoupling from leaderboard bias. We recommend that reporting LPP alongside benchmarks provides a deeper, interpretable understanding of model behavior, enabling more reliable model selection, safety assessment, and evaluation beyond surface-level accuracy.

</details>


### [202] [Recovering Diversity Without Losing Alignment: A DPO Recipe for Post-Trained LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30021)
*Vinay Samuel,Yapei Chang,Mohit Iyyer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: REDIPO是一种离线DPO数据构建流程，能从基座模型中恢复多种有效的回答模式，在保持对齐收益的同时提升LLM输出的多样性。在多个模型上，NoveltyBench distinct_k提升134%、33%、44%，且MTBench、IFEval、Arena-Hard性能基本维持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放式指令通常有多个有效答案，用户能从多种回答中受益，但后训练（post-training）往往将LLM的输出空间收窄到一小部分规范回答上，限制了输出的多样性。

Method: REDIPO流程包括：(1) 从基座模型和指令模型中对每个提示采样回答；(2) 用指令模型重写基座模型的回答；(3) 过滤候选回答以保证安全性和指令遵循质量；(4) 构建偏好对，在指令遵循奖励相似的候选回答中，优先选择具有边际多样性的回答。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B、OLMo-3-7B和LLaMA-3.1-8B上，NoveltyBench distinct_k分别提升134%、33%、44%；DivPO多样性变化为0%、-6%、-4%；MTBench、IFEval、Arena-Hard性能基本维持；HarmBench攻击成功率降低。

Conclusion: 基座模型生成的多样化有效回答可以通过精心构建的偏好数据重新引入到后训练模型中，同时保持对齐收益。边际多样性配对和基座回答重写是多样性提升的关键驱动因素，过滤和质量边界配对有助于保持对齐。

Abstract: Many open-ended instructions have multiple valid answers that users can benefit from seeing, but post-training often narrows an LLM's output space toward a small set of canonical responses. We introduce REDIPO, an offline DPO data-construction pipeline for recovering distinct valid answer modes while preserving the alignment benefits of the instruct model. For each prompt, REDIPO samples responses from both base and instruct models, rewrites base-model responses with the instruct model, filters candidates for safety and instruction-following quality, and builds preference pairs that favor marginally diverse responses among candidates with similar instruction-following reward. Across Qwen3-4B, OLMo-3-7B, and LLaMA-3.1-8B, REDIPO improves NoveltyBench distinct_k by 134%, 33%, and 44% relative to the instruct checkpoints, while DivPO changes diversity by 0%, -6%, and -4% on the same models. These gains largely maintain MTBench, IFEval, and Arena-Hard performance, and reduce direct-category HarmBench attack success rate. Ablations show that marginal-diversity pair selection and base-response rewriting drive the diversity gains, while filtering and quality-bounded pairing help maintain alignment. Overall, our results show that diverse valid answers from base-model generations can be reintroduced through carefully constructed preference data while retaining the alignment benefits of post-training. We release our code and data at https://github.com/vsamuel2003/RiDiPO.

</details>


### [203] [Give it Space! Explicit Disentangling of Positional and Semantic Representations in Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30022)
*Pierre-Antoine Lequeu,Camille Barboule,Benjamin Piwowarski*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文通过解耦位置编码与语义信息的处理方法，发现绝对位置信息在Transformer中自发坍缩为低频二维流形，相对位置仅支持语义注意力头，而标准位置编码在MLM压力下丢失宏观结构。解耦方法在65项语言现象中的49项上提升了表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有位置编码方法（如RoPE）在长上下文理解和检索任务中仍存在困难，而位置信息在Transformer内部的处理和存储机制尚不清晰。理解内部位置机制有助于设计更好的位置编码。

Method: 基于位置信号与语义信号在训练好的Transformer中占据近似正交子空间的证据，修改编码器Transformer以处理三个明确解耦的信息流：语义、绝对位置（AP）和相对位置（RP），并将掩码语言建模（MLM）目标限制在语义流上。

Result: (1) 孤立AP子空间自发坍缩为捕获文档结构的低频二维流形；(2) 注意力头分化为结构导向和语义导向两组，RP仅支持后者；(3) 标准位置编码不能鲁棒地保留宏观结构：RoPE和RP仅弱编码，纠缠AP在MLM压力下在最后层丢失该结构。解耦方法在Flash-Holmes探测基准的65项语言现象中的49项上提升了语言表示。

Conclusion: 解耦的位置信息处理方法能更好地保留位置编码，改善语言表示，为设计更优的位置编码提供了 mechanistic 理解和设计思路。

Abstract: Positional encoding (PE) underpins how permutation-invariant Transformers represent sequence order, yet how positional information is processed and stored remains poorly understood. Modern PE methods such as RoPE still struggle on tasks such as long-context understanding or retrieval \cite{chen-etal-2025-hope}. Hence, a better understanding of the internal positional mechanism could help design better PE. Building on evidence that positional and semantic signals occupy nearly orthogonal subspaces in trained Transformers, we modify an encoder Transformer to process three explicitly disentangled streams: semantic, absolute positional (AP) and relative positional (RP), and confine the masked-language-modeling (MLM) objective to the semantic stream. This decoupling enables a clean mechanistic study and yields three take-aways. (1) The isolated AP subspace spontaneously collapses into a low-frequency two-dimensional manifold that captures the structure of the document; (2) Attention heads specialize into structure and semantic-oriented groups, with RP exclusively supporting the latter; (3) Standard positional encodings do not robustly retain macroscopic structure: RoPE and RP only weakly encode it, and entangled AP loses it in the final layers under MLM pressure. The disentangled approach preserves positional encoding, which improves linguistic representation on 49 of the 65 linguistic phenomena of the Flash-Holmes probing benchmark.

Method: UniSteer学习一个在激活空间中的通用条件速度场，通过流反转将源激活部分传输到潜在状态，再在目标文本条件下重新生成并注入回冻结的LLM中；同时支持通过选择重构能量最低的文本标签进行激活空间分类。

Abstract: Activation-based control steers large language models (LLMs) by intervening on their internal representations during inference, and has emerged as an effective paradigm for controlling behaviors such as persona and style. However, existing methods often rely on fixed steering directions or task-specific intervention modules, making them difficult to adapt to fine-grained concepts and compositional constraints. We propose UniSteer, a text-guided activation flow matching model that learns a conditional distribution over residual-stream activations from natural-language conditions. Instead of fitting a separate intervention for each target behavior, UniSteer learns a universal conditional velocity field in activation space. At inference time, UniSteer performs flow inversion by partially transporting a source activation toward a latent state and regenerating it under a target textual condition before injecting it back into the frozen LLM. The same conditional model supports activation-space classification by selecting the textual label with the lowest reconstruction energy. Experiments on three target LLMs show that UniSteer provides a unified interface across behavioral control, truthfulness steering, fine-grained concept steering, multi-constraint instruction following, and activation-space classification.

In this paper, we propose Adaptive Targeted Dynamic Chunking (ATDC), a novel byte-compression control mechanism designed to enhance the effectiveness of dynamic chunking within hierarchical architectures. Our approach utilizes curriculum learning to progressively adjust the compression ratio during training, transitioning from low to high compression to stabilize the learning process. We provide an analysis establishing the relationship between the target compression ratio and Bytes-Per-Innermost-Chunk (BPIC), allowing for tracking of chunk-size evolution throughout the training phase. Evaluations conducted on the FineWeb-Edu 100B dataset demonstrate that hierarchical models equipped with ATDC achieve competitive Bits-Per-Byte (BPB) performance compared to conventional baselines operating at both byte and token levels. Furthermore, the proposed method exhibits more stable training dynamics and superior final performance across diverse downstream tasks compared to models using fixed compression ratios, while maintaining the inherent robustness and flexibility of byte-level processing.

### [209] [SEAL: Can Saturated Benchmarks Be Revived by LLM-as-a-Meta-Judge?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30104)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Rather than constructing harder alternatives, we ask whether existing tasks can be made informative again through improved evaluation over the same candidate outputs. Therefore, we present Seeded Elimination with Adaptive LLM-as-a-Meta-Judge, a self-improving evaluation protocol for extracting latent ranking signal from saturated benchmarks. SEAL seeds candidate outputs into a single elimination and evaluates each match with task-level principles plus self-improving checklist criteria. We evaluate SEAL on multiple saturated benchmarks covering code generation, mathematical reasoning, knowledge-intensive question answering, and tool-use agent task completion. Across these settings, SEAL improves the ranking-accuracy--latency trade-off over competing protocols, attaining 0.83--1.00 Spearman agreement with full pairwise judging and 4/4 top-1 agreement, while requiring only 11.89 calls per task compared with 28.00 for full pairwise evaluation.

Motivation: 现有放射学报告生成（RRG）通常采用单路径解码生成单一报告作为最终输出，但观察到固定MLLM在候选池中常生成比默认解码更优的报告，说明推理时决策是未被充分探索的瓶颈。

Method: CCS框架包含两步：首先采样多个候选报告（rollout pool），然后通过一个融合文本效用和放射学适配效用的联合评分函数选择最佳报告。其中放射学适配效用由基于图像-报告训练的多模态嵌入器计算，衡量候选报告间超越表面文本相似性的临床一致性。

Result: 在三个数据集和多个放射学MLLM上，CCS一致优于单路径解码和通用Best-of-N基线，在临床指标上提升尤为显著。消融实验验证了图像引导效用提供了独立于文本共识的选择维度，并表明推理时RRG仍有较大提升空间。

Conclusion: CCS作为一种轻量级、与解码器无关的推理时选择方法，能有效提升RRG临床质量，且不依赖额外训练或数据扩展，揭示了推理时优化在医学影像报告生成中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Radiology report generation (RRG) is commonly formulated as a single-path generation task, where a multimodal large language model (MLLM) produces one decoded report as the final output. While recent progress has largely been driven by scaling training data, model capacity, and retrieval mechanisms, improving report quality at inference time remains underexplored. In this work, we observe that fixed radiology MLLMs often generate clinically stronger reports elsewhere in their candidate pool than the one selected by default decoding, suggesting that inference-time decision making remains an overlooked bottleneck. To address this, we propose Clinical Consensus Selection (CCS), a decoder-agnostic inference-time selection framework that samples multiple candidate reports and selects the one with the highest clinical consensus across the rollout pool. CCS unifies text-based utilities with a radiology-adapted utility computed by an image--report-trained multimodal embedder, which measures candidate agreement beyond surface-level textual similarity. Across three datasets and multiple radiology MLLMs, CCS consistently improves inference-time performance over single-path decoding and generic Best-of-N baselines, with particularly clear gains on clinical metrics. Further analysis shows that image-grounded utility forms a selection axis distinct from textual consensus and that substantial headroom remains for improving RRG at inference time.

</details>

CorPipe 26 is an improved version of CorPipe 25, with a new variant predicting empty nodes together with mentions and coreference links in a single model. Our system outperforms all other submissions in the LLM track by 2.8 percent points and all submissions in the unconstrained track by 9.5 percent points. Furthermore, we perform a series of ablation experiments with different model sizes, empty node prediction methods, and cross-lingual zero-shot evaluation. ### [213] [GRUFF: LLM Pronoun Fidelity, Reasoning, and Biases in German](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30214)
*Fabian Mewes,Anne Lauscher,Vagrant Gautam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文构建了德语的GRUFF数据集，系统评估了大语言模型在四种性别一致系统和新代词上的指代忠实性，发现模型对阳性/阴性名词有强语法一致能力但对新代词表现弱，且易受干扰项影响，职业刻板印象在不同语法格和模型间相关性差。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了名为GRUFF的大规模数据集，覆盖四种不同的名词性别一致系统（阳/阴/中/新代词xier和en），以及四组代词。通过该数据集测试LLM在有无干扰项条件下的指代忠实性，并分析职业刻板印象在不同语法格之间的相关性。

Result: LLM在无显式语境时对阳性和阴性实体表现出强语法一致性，但对新代词xier和en表现不佳；模型总体上对干扰项不鲁棒，但encoder-only模型在德语中比英语更鲁棒，反映了语法性别的重要性；职业刻板印象在不同语法格之间相关性差，除架构相近的模型外。

Conclusion: 德语中语法性别对模型指代推理有重要影响；现有模型在包容性新代词上仍有不足；职业刻板印象在语法格间不一致，提示评估偏差需多维度进行。

Abstract: Third-person singular pronouns have long been used to study stereotypical biases in language models and to test their abilities to reason about reference. More recently, the interplay between reasoning and bias has been investigated with the task of pronoun fidelity, which assesses models' abilities to correctly reuse a previously-specified pronoun for a discourse entity, independent of other potentially distracting discourse entities mentioned in between. However, such research focuses on English, which is a language with limited grammatical gender and almost no gender agreement. In this paper we contribute a novel, large-scale dataset, GRUFF, to measure pronoun fidelity in German, covering four different gender agreement systems in nouns, and four sets of pronouns. With this dataset, we show that LLMs show strong grammatical agreement for masculine and feminine entities in the absence of explicit context, but not for neopronouns xier and en. Models are generally not robust to distractors, but encoder-only models are more robust in German than in English, reflecting the importance of grammatical gender. Finally, we show that occupational stereotypes in this context are poorly correlated across grammatical cases, and across most models, except ones with closely related architectures. We release all code and data to encourage further work on gender-inclusive language and referential reasoning in German.

### [214] [Do Language Models Track Entities Across State Changes?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30233)
*Zilu Tang,Qiao Zhao,Gabriel Franco,Derry Wijaya,Aaron Mueller,Sebastian Schuster,Najoung Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究复杂自然语言场景下，Transformer语言模型如何实现实体追踪（Entity Tracking）。发现模型并非逐步、增量式地追踪世界状态，而是在查询变得明确时，于最后一个token处并行聚合相关信息。特别地，REMOVE操作通过全局抑制标签（global suppression tag）实现，该机制脆弱且可预测多种失败模式，作者通过消融该标签部分缓解了问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要探讨无状态变化下的实体绑定机制，但对复杂度更高、涉及多次状态变更的自然语言实体追踪问题理解有限，亟需揭示非玩具级LM在该场景下的工作机制。

Method: 通过行为实验和机制分析相结合的方式，探究LM在PUT、REMOVE、MOVE等操作下的实体追踪机制。发现模型采用非增量式策略，在查询出现时于最后一层token处并行聚合信息；识别出REMOVE操作依赖全局抑制标签，并通过机制性干预验证其因果作用。

Result: 1) LM并非增量追踪状态，而是延迟到查询token出现时并行处理；2) REMOVE操作采用脆弱全局抑制机制，而非精准删除；3) 该机制可预测多种行为失败模式并得到验证；4) 通过消融全局抑制标签可部分修复该问题。

Conclusion: LM解决了一个本质上顺序的任务却采用非顺序策略，揭示了行为分析与机制分析相互促进的研究范式：行为结果启发机制假设，机制分析预测行为失败模式，从而指导更完善的行为评估。

Abstract: Entity tracking (ET), the ability to keep track of states, is a fundamental skill that underlies complex reasoning. An increasing amount of work investigates how transformer language models (LMs) solve entity binding $\textit{without}$ state changes. However, there is limited understanding of how non-toy LMs address ET problems of realistic difficulties expressed in natural language. To this end, we investigate the mechanisms underlying ET in more complex scenarios featuring multiple state-changing operations. We find that LMs do not incrementally track world states across tokens or query-relevant states across layers, but simply aggregate relevant information in parallel at the last token when the query becomes evident. We further investigate mechanisms of individual operations ($\texttt{PUT}$, $\texttt{REMOVE}$, $\texttt{MOVE}$) to characterize this non-incremental ET mechanism. Surprisingly, LMs implement the $\texttt{REMOVE}$ operation with a fragile global suppression tag; this global removal mechanism predicts various failure modes that we confirm behaviorally. We provide a mechanistic solution of nullifying this tag to partially address this issue. Overall, our findings reveal that LMs solve a fundamentally sequential task using a non-sequential strategy. More broadly, our work illustrates how behavioral and mechanistic analyses can fruitfully interact. Behavioral results inform mechanistic hypotheses, and insights from mechanistic analyses help build stronger behavioral evaluations by predicting failure modes missing from existing evaluations.

</details>

Result: 封闭输入验证仍具挑战；联网搜索带来最大性能提升；LLM的源选择策略与人类社区笔记评审者的共识系统性偏离；跨语言-领域切片及证据生态系统存在显著差异。

Abstract: Misinformation verification increasingly occurs in public, fast-moving, and multilingual online settings, where static benchmarks provide an incomplete measure of model reliability. This release contains 15,992 standalone claims across five languages and two domains. We evaluate ten LLMs under varying inference-time capabilities, including thinking and web-search. Our results show that closed-input verification remains challenging, web access yields the largest gains, and web-enabled LLMs' source-selection policies are systematically misaligned with the sources human Community Notes raters converge on -- a gap that closes through model-specific mechanisms of retrieval expansion or pruning. We further find substantial variation across language-domain slices and across the evidence ecosystems used by web-enabled systems. Beyond evaluation, CommunityFact positions Community Notes as a training signal for claim-conditioned source suggesters that could improve factual verification on novel claims.

### [216] [Knowing What to Solve Before How: Preplan Empowered LLM Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30245)
*Shaojie Wang,Liang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PPC（Preplan-Plan-CoT）框架在传统的 问题→规划→思维链 范式基础上，引入显式的预规划阶段（preplan），形成 问题→预规划→规划→思维链 的新范式，通过在两端确保预规划的概念完整性（含spoiler-score检测器和复合GRPO奖励），在四个基座模型和五个数学推理基准上取得了40个指标中39个最优的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于规划的推理方法（问题→规划→思维链）存在范式层面的固有缺陷：规划阶段和执行阶段都只关注"如何解决问题"，而"解决什么问题"——即识别问题类型、适用的工具以及可预见的陷阱——完全隐式处理，缺乏明确的认知环节。

Method: 提出PPC框架，核心创新包括：(1) 引入显式的预规划（preplan）阶段，形成问题→预规划→规划→思维链的新范式；(2) 设计三阶段合成流程，结合spoiler-score检测器过滤信息泄露和剧透故障，构建干净的预规划监督数据；(3) 采用复合GRPO奖励机制，强制生成的规划真正遵循预规划。

Result: 在四个基座模型和五个数学推理基准上，PPC在40个评估指标中取得39个最优结果，相比最强基线，maj@16提升+2.23，pass@16提升+3.06，且未引入额外推理token开销。

Conclusion: PPC通过显式的预规划阶段弥补了现有规划推理范式的认知缺失，在数学推理任务上取得显著且一致的性能提升，验证了"先明确解决什么问题，再规划如何解决"这一范式转换的有效性。

Abstract: Current plan-based reasoning methods improve large language models (LLMs) by inserting a planning stage before execution, giving rise to the question $\rightarrow$ plan $\rightarrow$ cot paradigm. While effective, a closer examination reveals an inherent paradigm-level gap: both the planning and its execution stages decide how to solve a problem, while the prior question of what to solve; recognizing the problem type, the applicable tools, and the foreseeable pitfalls; remains entirely implicit. To bridge this gap, we propose PPC (Preplan-Plan-CoT), a framework that introduces an explicit problem-understanding stage, the preplan, yielding a new question $\rightarrow$ preplan $\rightarrow$ plan $\rightarrow$ cot paradigm. Realizing this paradigm requires safeguarding the conceptual integrity of preplan at both ends. Specifically, we design a three-stage synthesis pipeline with a spoiler-score detector that filters out leakage and spoiler failures to build clean preplan supervision, and a composite GRPO reward enforces that the generated plan genuinely follows from the preplan. Experiments across four backbones and five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that PPC achieves the best results on 39 of 40 metrics, improving maj@16 and pass@16 by +2.23 and +3.06 over the strongest baseline without introducing additional inference token overhead.

</details>


### [217] [Same Evidence, Different Answers: Canonical-Context On-Policy Distillation for Multi-Turn Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30251)
*Zizhuo Lin,Quanling Liu,Jinsheng Quan,Chao Zhang,Yifan Zhu,Xing Shi,Jingtao Xu,Zhihui Li,Yawei Luo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLM在单次完整提示下表现良好，但在多轮对话中逐步呈现相同信息时性能下降，原因在于"自我锚定漂移"——部分信息下的回答引入无依据假设并扭曲最终答案。本文提出规范上下文在策略蒸馏（CCOPD），通过冻结教师模型（完整提示）训练学生模型（逐步信息），在数学对话上训练后，RAW-SHARDED性能平均相对提升32%，同时保持完整上下文性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在单次完整提示与多轮逐步呈现相同信息时存在显著的性能差距，作者认为核心原因是"自我锚定漂移"——模型在部分信息下生成回答时引入无依据的假设，这些假设在后继轮次中持续扭曲最终答案。

Method: 提出Canonical-Context On-Policy Distillation (CCOPD)：使用同一个基础模型的两个副本，冻结的教师模型以完整FULL prompt为条件，可训练的学生模型通过多轮对话逐步接收相同证据；CCOPD将学生模型在其自身轨迹上的行为与教师的规范完整上下文行为对齐。训练仅在数学问题对话上进行。

Result: 在数学及五个零样本域外任务族上，RAW-SHARDED性能平均相对提升32%，同时完整上下文性能基本保持。进一步分析表明CCOPD增强了模型对用户证据的依赖，降低了对前序助手轮次污染的敏感性。

Conclusion: CCOPD有效缓解了多轮对话中的自我锚定漂移问题，通过将增量信息的对话行为蒸馏对齐到完整上下文行为，显著提升了模型在逐步信息场景下的推理性能，且具有良好的跨域泛化能力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often solve a task when all instructions are given in a single prompt, but fail when the same information is revealed gradually across turns. When a clean FULL prompt and a RAW-SHARDED conversation contain the same complete user evidence, the model should still arrive at the same answer. We argue that a key reason for this gap is self-anchored drift: responses produced under partial information introduce unsupported assumptions, and those assumptions later distort the final answer. To reduce this effect, we propose Canonical-Context On-Policy Distillation (CCOPD). During training, the same base model is used in two roles: a frozen teacher conditioned on the clean FULL prompt and a trainable student that receives the same evidence incrementally through a multi-turn conversation; CCOPD aligns the student's behavior on its own trajectories with the teacher's canonical full-context behavior. Trained only on math problem conversations, CCOPD yields a 32\% average relative improvement in RAW-SHARDED performance over the original base model across math and five zero-shot out-of-domain task families, while largely preserving full-context performance. Further analyses suggest that CCOPD strengthens grounding in user evidence and reduces sensitivity to contamination from earlier assistant turns.

*Ziwen Xu,Haiwen Hong,Linsong Yu,Benglei Cui,Longtao Huang,Hui Xue,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出参数化记忆定律（Parametric Memory Law），揭示LoRA微调中损失减少与参数量的幂律关系，发现预测概率p>0.5是贪婪解码下逐字回忆的充分条件，并基于此提出MemFT阈值引导优化策略，通过动态分配训练预算提升记忆保真度和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要依赖定性下游评估，缺乏对LoRA在连续学习中精确参数化记忆的量化容量上限和底层动态的理解。

Method: 将LoRA作为潜空间内的可控记忆容量探针，系统量化精确参数化记忆；提出参数化记忆定律（幂律关系）；进行token级细粒度分析发现相变条件（p>0.5）；提出MemFT阈值引导优化策略动态分配训练预算。

Result: 验证了参数化记忆定律的幂律关系；发现p>0.5是贪婪解码下逐字回忆的充分条件；MemFT在记忆保真度和效率上优于基线。

Conclusion: 提出的参数化记忆定律和MemFT策略为LLM在动态环境中的高效知识更新提供了理论依据和实用方法。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) must continuously learn and update knowledge to remain effective in dynamic real-world environments. While Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) is widely used for such memory updates, existing studies mainly rely on qualitative downstream evaluations, leaving the quantitative capacity limits and underlying dynamics of exact parametric memory largely unexplored. To bridge this gap, we employ LoRA as a controlled memory capacity probe within the latent space to systematically quantify exact parametric memory. We introduce the Parametric Memory Law, a robust power law linking loss reduction Delta L to effective parameters and sequence length. At the token level, fine-grained analysis reveals a deterministic phase transition, demonstrating that a prediction probability of p > 0.5 constitutes a sufficient condition for verbatim recall under greedy decoding. Driven by these insights, we introduce MemFT, a threshold-guided optimization strategy that dynamically redistributes the training budget toward sub-threshold tokens. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that MemFT can enhance memory fidelity and efficiency. Code will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/ParametricMemoryLaw.

### [219] [Loong: A Human-Like Long Document Translation Agent with Observe-and-Act Adaptive Context Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30274)
*Yutong Wang,Xuebo Liu,Derek F. Wong,Zhilin Li,Rongqing Jiang,Min Zhang,Shimin Tao,Daimeng Wei,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Loong，一种类人长文档翻译智能体，通过3E记忆模块（精华-样例-实体）存储摘要、句对和实体记录，并利用强化学习优化上下文选择策略，在英⇄中、德、法三个方向平均提升13.0个翻译质量分数，展现出强泛化性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在文档级翻译中面临双重挑战：有限上下文窗口导致全局连贯性不足，而冗余上下文信息又降低了翻译质量。现有方法被动地注意所有历史信息，无法有效筛选最优上下文。

Method: 提出Loong智能体，包含3E记忆模块（Essence精华摘要、Exemplar样例句对、Entity实体记录）以结构化存储历史上下文；通过深度推理自适应识别最优翻译指导上下文；利用强化学习（基于自身采样的观察-行动推理轨迹生成的偏好数据）优化上下文选择策略。

Result: 在英⇄中、德、法三个翻译方向上，Loong在三个评估指标上平均提升13.0分；展现出跨领域泛化能力和对上下文噪声的鲁棒性；在超长文档翻译中保持出色的稳定性。

Conclusion: Loong通过模仿人类翻译策略（选择性关注关键记忆）和强化学习优化，有效解决了长文档翻译中上下文选择的核心难题，为文档级机器翻译提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Document-level translation remains one of the most challenging tasks for large language models, which are constrained by limited context windows that impede global cohesion, while simultaneously suffering from redundant contextual information that degrades translation quality. To address this, we propose a human-like long document translation agent called Loong, which leverages a 3E memory module (Essence-Exemplar-Entity) to store summaries, sentence pairs, and entity records as historical context. Instead of passively attending to all history, Loong performs deep reasoning to adaptively identify the optimal context for translation guidance. Loong optimizes its context policy through reinforcement learning, utilizing preference data derived from its own sampled observe-and-act reasoning trajectories. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that Loong achieves substantial translation quality improvements in English $\Leftrightarrow$ Chinese, German, and French directions, with average gains of up to 13.0 points across the three evaluation metrics. Furthermore, Loong exhibits strong generalization across domains and robustness against contextual noise, while maintaining remarkable stability in ultra-long document translation. Our code is released at https://github.com/YutongWang1216/LoongDocMT.

</details>


### [220] [MedCase-Structured: A Text-to-FHIR Dataset for Benchmarking Diagnostic Reasoning in Clinically Realistic EHR Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30295)
*Valentina Bui Muti,Eugénie Dulout,Ziquan Fu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从非结构化文本生成符合临床标准（HL7 FHIR R4）的结构化数据管线的pipeline，用于构建更真实的临床决策支持系统评估基准。在MedCaseReasoning基础上构建了MedCase-Structured数据集，82.5%的案例成功生成有效FHIR数据。评估发现，LLMs在结构化FHIR输入上的诊断准确率低于纯文本，强调了部署对齐的基准测试的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM临床评估基准多依赖静态数据集或非结构化输入，无法反映临床系统中使用的结构化、可互操作的数据格式，缺乏与现实电子健康记录一致的评价环境。

Method: 提出一个pipeline，结合分阶段LLM生成与术语接地验证修复机制，从非结构化文本生成符合HL7 FHIR R4标准的临床数据，减少幻觉代码并确保结构与语义一致性。应用于MedCaseReasoning构建MedCase-Structured数据集。

Result: 82.5%的案例成功生成有效FHIR bundle；在MedCase-Structured上评估发现，LLMs在结构化FHIR输入上的诊断准确率低于纯文本输入。

Conclusion: 部署对齐的基准测试对于准确评估LLM在临床场景中的表现至关重要，结构化数据格式的引入揭示了纯文本评估无法发现的性能差异。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) show promise for clinical reasoning and decision support, but evaluation in realistic, electronic health record-congruent settings remains limited. Existing benchmarks often rely on static datasets or unstructured inputs that do not reflect the structured, interoperable data formats used in clinical systems. We introduce a pipeline for generating clinically realistic HL7 FHIR R4 bundles from unstructured text, enabling controllable evaluation of clinical decision support systems. The pipeline combines staged LLM generation with terminology-grounded validation and repair to reduce hallucinated codes and enforce structural and semantic consistency. Applying this approach to MedCaseReasoning, we construct MedCase-Structured, a synthetic dataset aligned with clinician-authored diagnostic cases, achieving valid FHIR generation for 82.5% of cases. Evaluation on MedCase-Structured reveals consistently lower diagnostic accuracy for LLMs on structured FHIR inputs than with plain text, highlighting the importance of deployment-aligned benchmarking.

### [221] [Resolution Diagnostics for Paired LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30315)
*Anany Kotawala*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现两个主流LLM排行榜中大量配对排名未达到常规配对检验的统计功效标准，并将配对LLM评估形式化为假设检验问题，提出分辨率比率q=N/N*作为核心诊断指标。研究揭示了广泛使用的未配对Cohen-h-plus-(1-rho)捷径方法在接近比较区间存在约两倍的偏差，且多数现成计算器继承此缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM排行榜的配对排名缺乏严格的统计检验支撑，可能导致不准确的结论和误导性排名，亟需建立规范的统计推断框架来评估LLM性能比较的可靠性。

Method: 将配对LLM评估建模为假设检验问题，基于水平α、功效(1-β)的检验反转，提出每对分辨率比率q=N/N*作为诊断指标；推导了小效应量下的二阶近似展开式，揭示未配对Cohen-h-plus-(1-rho)捷径的偏差。

Result: Open LLM Leaderboard v1中11/40的配对比较和MMLU-Pro中4/9（聚类后6/9）的相邻排名对在(α,1-β)=(0.05,0.8)下未达到分辨率目标；未配对捷径方法偏差约2倍；多数现成计算器（Cohen 1988, G*Power, R pwr）继承此偏差。

Conclusion: 当前LLM排行榜的统计严谨性不足，广泛使用的未配对功效分析方法存在系统性偏差；该模式在多重比较校正和任意有效序贯检验下仍然存在，表明需要更严格的统计框架来评估LLM性能比较。

Abstract: Across two public LLM leaderboards, many displayed pairwise rankings do not meet a conventional paired-test resolution target under the actual paired evaluation design: 11 of 40 Open LLM Leaderboard v1 pairwise comparisons and 4 of 9 MMLU-Pro top-10 adjacent-rank pairs are unresolved at (alpha, 1-beta) = (0.05, 0.8). The MMLU-Pro count rises to 6/9 under real subject-level clustering and stays at 5-6 out of 9 in 99.9% of category-bootstrap resamples. We frame paired LLM evaluation as a hypothesis-testing problem, invert level-alpha, power-(1-beta) tests, and report a per-pair resolution ratio q = N/N* as the primary diagnostic. A sharp small-effect expansion with an explicit second-order constant shows that the widely-used unpaired Cohen-h-plus-(1-rho) shortcut deviates from the correct N* by approximately a factor of two in the close-comparison regime, a deficit that three of five off-the-shelf calculators(Cohen 1988, G*Power, R pwr) silently inherit when the user post-multiplies their per-arm output by (1-rho). The unresolved-pair pattern remains under multiplicity correction and anytime-valid sequential testing.

</details>


### [222] [COMPOSE: Composing Future Theorems from Citations and Formal Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30333)
*David Busbib,Michael Werman*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出COMPOSE框架，通过结合科学引文图和形式化定理依赖图来生成合理的未来数学定理声明，实验表明该方法优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅建模引文方向或形式化依赖中的一种约束，生成的数学声明要么缺乏充分依据，要么动机不足。本文旨在同时满足这两个约束，生成更合理、更丰富的未来数学定理。

Method: 提出COMPOSE（双图框架），将语言模型同时条件于科学引文上下文和形式化定理结构。构建了包含108K个配对科学-形式图示例的数据集（来自arXiv和Mathlib），以及47K个2024-2025年未来论文的基准。

Result: COMPOSE在检索真实未来论文任务上优于强基线，在LLM评判下取得最佳整体性能，生成更扎实且数学上更丰富的输出。

Conclusion: 未来数学声明生成受益于科学上下文与形式化结构的结合。

Abstract: A plausible future mathematical claim must satisfy two constraints: it should follow the direction of prior work and respect the formal dependencies that constrain what can validly follow. Existing approaches typically model only one of these sources, producing claims that are either weakly grounded or insufficiently motivated. We introduce grounded future mathematical generation, where the goal is to generate a plausible future theorem-like claim for an anchor paper using two complementary sources of context: its scientific citation graph and aligned formal theorem dependency graph. To address this setting, we propose COMPOSE, a dual-graph framework that conditions a language model on both scientific citation context and formal theorem structure. To support this setting, we construct a dataset of 108K paired scientific-formal graph examples from arXiv and Mathlib, together with a benchmark of 47K future papers from 2024--2025. Experiments show that COMPOSE outperforms strong baselines on retrieval to real future papers and achieves the best overall performance under LLM-judge evaluation, producing more grounded and mathematically richer outputs. These results show that future mathematical generation benefits from combining scientific context with formal structure. Project page is available at https://david-busbib.github.io/COMPOSE-page/.

### [223] [Unlocking the Working Memory of Large Language Models for Latent Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30343)
*Lukas Aichberger,Sepp Hochreiter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出RiM（Reasoning in Memory）方法，用固定特殊token序列作为记忆块替代自回归推理步骤生成，实现大语言模型的潜在推理。该方法通过两阶段课程学习（先监督后自优化），在单次前向传播中完成计算，在多个推理基准上匹配或超越现有潜在推理方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型通过生成中间token来扩展测试时计算，但这将推理与自回归生成耦合，混淆了内部计算与外部通信。受人类认知中工作记忆可内部操作信息而不需外化中间思路的启发，本文旨在设计一种无需自回归生成中间步骤的潜在推理方法。

Method: RiM使用固定特殊token序列（记忆块）替代自回归生成的推理步骤，这些记忆块可在单次前向传播中处理。训练采用两阶段课程：第一阶段，在每块记忆块后预测显式推理步骤以建立语义关联；第二阶段，丢弃步骤级监督，在每块记忆块后迭代优化最终答案。

Result: 在多个推理基准上，RiM在不同系列和规模的语言模型中均匹配或超越了现有潜在推理方法，同时避免了自回归生成思维链。

Conclusion: 大语言模型可以通过训练利用工作记忆作为有效的潜在推理机制，用固定记忆块替代自回归生成，在计算效率与推理能力之间取得良好平衡。

Abstract: To improve the reasoning capabilities of large language models, test-time compute is typically scaled by generating intermediate tokens before the final answer. However, this couples reasoning to autoregressive generation and thereby conflates internal computation with external communication. In contrast, human cognition can use working memory to hold and manipulate information internally without the need to externalize intermediate thoughts. Drawing on this principle, we introduce Reasoning in Memory (RiM), a latent reasoning method that replaces the autoregressive generation of reasoning steps with memory blocks. These memory blocks are fixed sequences of special tokens that unlock the working-memory capacity of large language models. Since they are fixed rather than generated, they can be processed in a single forward pass, enabling compute-efficient latent reasoning. To operationalize these memory blocks, we employ a two-stage curriculum. First, we ground them by predicting explicit reasoning steps after each memory block. Second, we discard this step-level supervision and iteratively refine the final answer after each memory block. Our experiments on reasoning benchmarks show that, across language models of different families and sizes, RiM matches or exceeds existing latent reasoning methods while avoiding the autoregressive generation of thoughts. These results demonstrate that large language models can be trained to use working memory as an effective mechanism for latent reasoning.

</details>


### [224] [LLMSurgeon: Diagnosing Data Mixture of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30348)
*Yaxin Luo,Jiacheng Cui,Xiaohan Zhao,Xinyi Shang,Jiacheng Liu,Xinyue Bi,Zhaoyi Li,Zhiqiang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出数据混合手术（DMS）框架，仅通过目标LLM生成的文本即可估计其预训练语料的领域分布。作者设计了LLMSurgeon方法，利用校准的软混淆矩阵解决逆问题，并构建了LLMScan验证套件，在开源模型上实现了高保真度的领域混合恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的预训练数据混合构成其"数字DNA"，但这一组成极少被公开，导致事后审计数据组合或来源变得困难。现有方法无法仅从生成的文本中有效恢复预训练数据的领域分布。

Method: 将数据混合手术形式化为标签偏移假设下的逆问题，LLMSurgeon通过估计校准的软混淆矩阵，求解带约束的逆问题来纠正系统性的领域混淆，从而恢复潜在的混合先验分布。

Result: 在基于开源LLM构建的LLMScan验证套件上，LLMSurgeon在固定协议下能够以高保真度恢复领域混合分布。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种实用的、事后的方法来审计基础模型的"数字DNA"，而无需访问其训练数据，为LLM数据组成的透明性提供了重要工具。

Abstract: The pretraining data mixture of Large Language Models (LLMs) constitutes their "digital DNA", shaping model behaviors, capabilities, and failure modes. Yet this composition is rarely disclosed, making post-hoc auditing of data combination or provenance difficult. In this work, we formalize $\textbf{Data Mixture Surgery (DMS)}$: given only generated text from a target LLM, estimate the domain-level distribution of its pretraining corpus under a predefined taxonomy. We propose $\textbf{LLMSurgeon}$, a strong framework that casts DMS as an inverse problem under the label-shift assumption. Rather than directly aggregating classifier outputs, LLMSurgeon estimates a calibrated $\textit{soft}$ confusion matrix and solves a constrained inverse problem to correct systematic domain confusion and recover the latent mixture prior. To evaluate, we introduce $\textbf{LLMScan}$, a recipe-verifiable evaluation suite built from open-source LLMs with transparent pretraining mixtures. Across LLMScan, LLMSurgeon recovers domain mixtures with high fidelity under fixed protocols. Our work presents a practical, post-hoc approach for auditing the digital DNA of foundation models without access to their training data.

</details>

### [225] [Behavior-Induced Mirror-Prox Temporal-Difference Learning for Faster Off-Policy Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28849)
*Xingguo Chen,Yuchen Shen,Shangdong Yang,Chao Li,Guang Yang,Wenhao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于行为策略诱导度量的Mirror-Prox时序差分方法STHTD-MP，用行为策略Bellman矩阵的对称部分替代协方差度量，在标准随机逼近假设下证明了其收敛性，并在多个基准上验证了其优于GTD2-MP的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有梯度时序差分方法中，辅助变量度量对实际性能影响显著。Mirror-Prox TD方法通常使用特征协方差度量，而混合TD方法表明行为策略转移信息能提供更具信息量的更新几何结构。本文旨在利用行为策略诱导的度量改进Mirror-Prox方法的鞍点几何结构。

Method: 提出STHTD-MP方法，在原始-对偶鞍点公式中，用行为策略Bellman矩阵的对称部分替换协方差度量；对原始变量和辅助变量使用单一学习率；对混合鞍点算子应用Mirror-Prox预测-校正步骤。

Result: 在标准随机逼近假设下建立了形式化收敛性分析（行为诱导度量正定、联合均值系统Hurwitz、Lyapunov有界性、ODE方法收敛）；推导了投影oracle遍历间隙界和精确均值算子比较（与GTD2-MP基于谱半径）；在二状态、Random Walk和Boyan Chain基准上验证了STHTD-MP有更小的均值收缩因子；Baird反例被识别为奇异边界情况。

Conclusion: 当行为诱导度量改善鞍点几何时，STHTD-MP可比GTD2-MP具有更小的均值收缩因子，从而获得更优的收敛性能。

Abstract: Gradient temporal-difference methods provide stable off-policy prediction with linear function approximation, but their practical performance is strongly affected by the geometry induced by the auxiliary-variable metric. Existing Mirror-Prox TD methods typically use the feature covariance metric, whereas hybrid TD methods suggest that behavior-policy transition information can provide a more informative update geometry. This paper proposes a behavior-induced Mirror-Prox temporal-difference method, called STHTD-MP, which replaces the covariance metric in the primal-dual saddle-point formulation with the symmetric part of the behavior-policy Bellman matrix. The method keeps a single learning rate for the primal and auxiliary variables and applies a Mirror-Prox prediction-correction step to the resulting hybrid saddle-point operator. We provide a formal convergence analysis for fixed-policy linear prediction under standard stochastic approximation assumptions: the behavior-induced metric is positive definite, the joint mean system is Hurwitz, boundedness follows from a Lyapunov argument, and the stochastic recursion converges by the ODE method. We further derive projected-oracle ergodic gap bounds and an exact mean-operator comparison with GTD2-MP based on the spectral radius of the deterministic Mirror-Prox error matrix. The analysis shows that STHTD-MP can have a smaller mean contraction factor than GTD2-MP when the behavior-induced metric improves the saddle-point geometry. Exact numerical mean-operator analysis on two-state, Random Walk, and Boyan Chain benchmarks supports this condition, while Baird's counterexample is identified as a singular boundary case where the strict assumptions fail.

</details>


### [226] [Behavior-Aware Auxiliary Corrections for Off-Policy Temporal-Difference Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28855)
*Xingguo Chen,Zhiang He,Yuchen Shen,Shangdong Yang,Chao Li,Guang Yang,Wenhao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将TDC中的辅助协方差矩阵替换为行为Bellman矩阵，得到BA-TDC和BA-TDRC算法，理论分析了其收敛性，实验表明行为感知的替换在某些任务上有益，但正则化对鲁棒性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离策略TD结合函数逼近时存在不稳定性问题。TDC通过辅助协方差校正来稳定离策略TD，但该辅助协方差的设计是否可以改进为行为感知的形式，以更好地适应离策略学习的几何结构，是一个待研究的问题。

Method: 在线性预测设置下，将TDC的辅助矩阵C替换为行为Bellman矩阵A_μ得到BA-TDC，再正则化得到BA-TDRC。给出有限状态均值系统公式，证明在Hurwitz稳定条件下的不动点保持和几乎必然收敛，通过谱半径比较确定性均值收敛速率。

Result: 在two-state counterexample、Baird's counterexample、Random Walk和Boyan Chain上的实验表明，行为感知替换在某些任务上本身就有显著收益，但在更难的任务上需要正则化才能保证鲁棒性能。

Conclusion: 行为感知的辅助几何结构替换是有益的设计方向，但正则化对于在更广泛困难设置下获得稳健性能是必要的。

Abstract: Temporal-difference learning with function approximation can be unstable under off-policy sampling. TDC stabilizes off-policy TD through an auxiliary covariance correction, and TDRC further regularizes this correction in a single-timescale recursion. This paper studies a behavior-aware replacement of the auxiliary covariance geometry in the linear prediction setting, which is the standard local model for understanding the feature-space dynamics of value-function approximation. We first replace the TDC auxiliary matrix (C) by the behavior Bellman matrix (A_μ), yielding BA-TDC, and then regularize the same behavior-aware equation to obtain BA-TDRC. This two-step construction separates the contribution of behavior-aware geometry from the contribution of regularization. The linear analysis also provides a tractable model for an auxiliary-geometry design question that arises in neural-network value approximation, where feature covariances and temporal transition matrices jointly shape the last-layer correction dynamics. We give a finite-state mean-system formulation, prove fixed-point preservation and almost-sure convergence under a Hurwitz stability condition on the instantiated mean system, and compare deterministic mean rates through the spectral radius of the exact linear error recursion. Experiments on the two-state counterexample, Baird's counterexample, Random Walk, and Boyan Chain show that the behavior-aware replacement can be highly beneficial by itself on some tasks, but that regularization is necessary for robust performance across harder settings.

</details>


### [227] [The Cognitive Categorical Transformer: Category-Theoretic Inductive Biases for Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28864)
*Al Kari*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CCT架构在GPT-2 Small基础上引入基于范畴论和认知科学的组件（尤其是GT-Full单纯复形消息传递），在WikiText-103上以21.27的验证困惑度超越GPT-2 Small的24.19，并通过消融实验将84%的提升归因于GT-Full，同时提出结构/一致性区分这一经验模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索认知科学和范畴论启发的组件能否在有限规模下提升语言模型的困惑度，并验证单纯复形消息传递这一拓扑结构对语言建模的实际贡献。

Method: 在306M参数的GPT-2 Small骨干上添加认知科学和范畴论启发的组件（包括GT-Full单纯复形消息传递等），采用匹配步数（215K步）、匹配数据和优化器的协议在WikiText-103上微调，并进行完整的消融实验。

Result: CCT达到21.27验证困惑度，相比GPT-2 Small基线（24.19）降低了2.92 PPL（12%相对改进）；消融实验表明GT-Full贡献了2.45 PPL（84%的改进）；而一致性类别的先验（sheaf平滑、adjunction往返、曲率正则化）均无效。

Conclusion: 首次通过消融实验验证了单纯复形消息传递能在306M参数规模上改善语言模型困惑度，并提出了结构/一致性区分：增加新拓扑结构的范畴先验能改善语言建模，而强制一致性恒等式的先验则不能。

Abstract: The Cognitive Categorical Transformer (CCT) is a 306M-parameter architecture that augments a pretrained GPT-2 Small backbone with cognitively grounded components derived from category theory and several inspirations from cognitive science. Under a matched-step protocol (215,000 optimizer steps, matched data, matched optimizer and schedule) on WikiText-103, CCT reaches 21.27 validation perplexity, compared with 24.19 for an identically fine-tuned GPT-2 Small baseline. The architecture therefore contributes a 2.92 PPL (12% relative) reduction beyond what in-domain fine-tuning alone provides. A retrain-from-scratch ablation that holds GT-Full simplicial message passing bypassed across the entire seven-phase activation schedule reaches 23.72 PPL, localizing 84% of the architectural improvement (2.45 of 2.92 PPL) to GT-Full. We present the first ablation-validated evidence that simplicial message passing improves language-model perplexity at the 306M-parameter scale on WikiText-103. Published GPT-2 Large reaches 22.05 zero-shot PPL on WikiText-103 with 6.2x more parameters than GPT-2 Small; this paper treats that number as an external published reference, not as the architectural benchmark. Three negative results on consistency-style categorical priors (sheaf smoothing, adjunction round-trip, curvature regularization) and the joint structural-prior result for GT-Full and PrecisionWeightedPP together support an empirical pattern termed the *structure/consistency distinction*, in which categorical priors that add new topology improve language modeling and those that enforce a consistency identity do not.

</details>

Abstract: Finite Element Analysis (FEA) serves as the cornerstone of modern engineering design. However, its workflow is inherently complex and relies heavily on domain expertise. To address these limitations, we propose VFEAgent, an end-to-end multi-agent system designed to automate FEA modeling and simulation directly from input images and problem descriptions. Our methodology integrates two core components: (1) a multimodal vision-language multi-agent pipeline that employs ReAct-driven reasoning to extract structured FEA specifications from heterogeneous inputs and (2) a verification-first code synthesis framework, incorporating robust self-debugging and fallback mechanisms to ensure executability and physical validity. We systematically evaluated the system across various engineering mechanics scenarios. The results demonstrate that VFEAgent achieves a high success rate in generating complete and physically valid simulations, outperforming LLM-based baseline methods in reliability and correctness. ### [229] [Review Arcade: On the Human Alignment and Gameability of LLM Reviews](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28897)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的论文评审正在被各大会议正式采用，但同时也存在作者利用LLM修改论文的情况。需要系统评估LLM评审与人类评审的一致性，以及作者"操纵"LLM评审的可能性。

Method: 基于2025年ACL Rolling Review(ARR)的论文数据进行实证实验，从审稿人和作者两个角度评估LLM评审：1) 比较LLM评审与人类评审的对齐程度；2) 测试不同提示词和模型的影响；3) 模拟作者迭代修改论文以迎合LLM评审的场景。

Result: LLM评审与人类评审的对齐有限（最佳情况下仅达到合理水平）；对齐程度在不同提示词和模型间差异显著；作者通过迭代修改可以显著提升评分，最多35%的论文可获统计显著的分数提升。

Conclusion: LLM评审存在被"博弈"的风险，作者可以利用迭代修改策略有效提升评分，这对学术评审的公正性构成潜在威胁。

Abstract: LLM-generated reviews for scientific papers are gaining considerable traction and are even being officially piloted by major conferences. We have to assume that not only reviewers are using LLM-assistance, but also that authors use LLMs to revise their papers before submitting. In this work, we perform empirical experiments on papers from the 2025 ACL Rolling Review (ARR) to evaluate LLM reviews from both the author and the reviewer perspective. First, we identify a limited alignment of LLM reviews with human ones. In the best-case scenario, the alignment is reasonable. However, we also find that LLM-human alignment varies substantially across prompts and models. Finally, we investigate the scenario in which the author uses an iterative draft-revise workflow to improve the submission according to the LLM review. We find that this "gaming" of LLM reviews can be effective in specific scenarios, leading to a statistically significant increase of overall scores for up to 35\% of papers. We publish our code: https://github.com/uhh-hcds/reviewarcade.

### [230] [Orthogonal Concept Erasure for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28902)
*Yuhao Sun,Lingyun Yu,Haoxiang Xu,Fengyuan Miao,Zhuoer Xu,Hongtao Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出正交概念擦除（OCE）方法，通过乘法性参数更新（正交变换）替代加法性更新，在扩散模型中实现精确的概念擦除同时保持整体生成能力，支持单概念和多概念擦除，速度可达4.3秒擦除100个概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于编辑的概念擦除方法依赖加法性参数更新，这不可避免地纠缠了神经元方向、幅度和角度几何，导致概念擦除与整体生成能力之间产生意外干扰，无法同时实现精确擦除和生成能力保持。

Method: 提出正交概念擦除（OCE），将编辑式擦除重建为乘法性参数更新：从几何视角应用逐层正交变换（闭式解），在擦除概念的同时保持神经元幅度和角度几何；针对多概念擦除中的冲突约束，引入子空间级目标与结构化子空间操作。

Result: 在单概念和多概念擦除任务中，OCE在擦除精度和非目标保持方面均优于现有方法，可在4.3秒内擦除多达100个概念。

Conclusion: 通过将参数更新从加法性改为乘法性（正交变换），OCE有效解耦了概念擦除与生成能力之间的冲突，为扩散模型概念擦除提供了一种高效、可扩展且部署友好的新范式。

Abstract: Concept erasure has emerged as a promising approach to mitigate undesired or unsafe content in diffusion models, yet existing methods still face significant limitations. While training-based methods are effective, their high computational cost limits scalability. Editing-based methods are more efficient and deployment-friendly, yet they struggle to simultaneously achieve precise concept erasure and preserve overall generative capacity. We identify this core limitation of the editing-based methods as reliance on additive parameter updates. Our empirical analysis reveals that concept semantics primarily depend on neuron direction rather than neuron magnitude, while overall generative capacity relies on the angular geometry of neurons. As additive updates inherently entangle direction, magnitude, and angular geometry, they inevitably introduce unintended interference between concept erasure and overall generation performance. To address this, we propose Orthogonal Concept Erasure (OCE), which reformulates editing-based erasure as multiplicative parameter updates from a geometric perspective. Specifically, OCE applies layer-wise orthogonal transformations derived from a closed-form solution to the parameters, enabling precise concept erasure while preserving the neuron magnitude and angular geometry. Furthermore, to address conflicting constraints in multi-concept erasure, OCE introduces a subspace-level objective with structured subspace manipulation, yielding a more effective and scalable erasure. Extensive experiments on single- and multi-concept erasure demonstrate that OCE outperforms existing methods in concept erasure and non-target preservation, erasing up to 100 concepts in 4.3 s. Code: https://github.com/HansSunY/OCE.

</details>

*Sara Metcalf,William Schoenberg*

Method: 采用开放式数字与组织基础设施，通过开源sd ai项目实现透明性和广泛贡献。设立指导组确定潜在基准优先级，技术组将基准实现为自动化测试。针对AI工具在定性建模、定量建模和模型讨论三类任务上实施多项评估测试，包括因果翻译、模型迭代、因果推理、一致性、模型行为解释、建模步骤建议和模型修复建议。

Abstract: AI tools to support real world decision making must be able to build simulation models that inform their recommendations and render them interpretable. Tools that can automate aspects of modeling practice must complement human expertise, not replace it. The BEAMS Initiative aims to guide the development of AI tools for modeling and simulation toward forms that are responsible and ethical by establishing benchmarks for human centered modeling and simulation practices. The initiative uses open digital and organizational infrastructure to collaboratively evaluate AI tools for modeling and simulation. The open source sd ai project hosted by the initiative establishes transparency and enables contributions to be shared broadly. A steering group focuses on prioritizing potential benchmarks, while a technical group focuses on implementing the benchmarks in the form of automated tests. Tests for several distinct categories of evaluation have been implemented and applied to AI tools that support qualitative model building, quantitative model building, and model discussion. These include tests for causal translation, model iteration, causal reasoning, conformance, model behavior explanation, suggested model building steps, and suggested model fixes. When engines from the sd ai project are coupled with different LLMs, their performance on these evaluations reveals variability across different AI tools. The evaluations implemented by the initiative demonstrate that AI enabled modeling tools perform better at discussion and basic qualitative tasks than with causal reasoning and quantitative error fixing. No single LLM dominates across engine types, highlighting the importance of specific tasks and tradeoffs between speed and accuracy. Ongoing efforts of the initiative aim to incorporate benchmarks that address concerns about bias by considering alternative perspectives and human centered use cases.

### [232] [Adopt $\neq$ Adapt: Longitudinal Analyses of LLM Conversations in the Wild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29018)
*Rebecca M. M. Hicke,Kiran Tomlinson*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 随机抽样约12,000名Microsoft Bing Copilot用户，分析其对话轨迹，并与WildChat-4.8M数据集进行对比。

Conclusion: 现有用户行为难以改变，且用户异质性显著；WildChat数据集存在严重偏差，下游使用时需谨慎。

Abstract: Although a growing body of research has begun to describe user--LLM interactions, the picture it paints is largely static; little is known about how individual users change their behavior over time. To address this gap, we analyze the conversational trajectories of $\sim$12,000 randomly sampled Microsoft Bing Copilot users and compare these with data from WildChat-4.8M. While the Copilot data contains significant population-level trends, we find that trends in individual user trajectories are much weaker; user habits prove to be overwhelmingly sticky. We also find stark differences between users of different activity levels: more active users have more successful conversations and use the LLM for more complex and professionally oriented tasks. Some user trends also appear in WildChat-4.8M, but we find evidence that this dataset is significantly skewed towards highly proficient "power" users. Ultimately, our results suggest that existing user behavior is difficult to change and demonstrate the extent of user heterogeneity. Our comparison between datasets highlights that WildChat does not represent typical user-AI interactions, an important caveat for downstream uses of the data.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
